 Sandhi
For the convenience of word search
internal and external
vowel Sandhis are decomposed by
eg vizeSaukti  vizeSokti
caiti  ceti
horAanyo  horAnyo
ko api  ko'pi
Consonantal sandhis are retained
 Compounds
Members of compound words are sometimes separated by
but not consistent
 Others
Varitants for the part beginning with  are supplied in

ṝc meṣe chakāro hibuke apy akāras
ṝd tule khakāro makare phakāraḥ
